*6	abraham lincoln february april american politician lawyer served 16th president united state march assassination april lincoln led united state civil war—its bloodiest war perhaps greatest moral constitutional political crisis preserved union paved way abolition slavery strengthened federal government modernized economy born hodgenville kentucky lincoln grew western frontier kentucky indiana largely selfeducated became lawyer illinois whig party leader elected illinois house representative served eight year elected united state house representative lincoln promoted rapid modernization economy bank tariff railroad originally agreed run second term congress opposition mexican–american war unpopular among illinois voter lincoln returned springfield resumed successful law practice reentering politics became leader building new republican party statewide majority illinois taking part series highly publicized debate opponent rival democrat stephen douglas lincoln spoke expansion slavery lost u senate race douglas lincoln secured republican party presidential nomination moderate swing state second choice grand majority convention delegate whose first choice due factionalism could garner enough vote win though gained little support slaveholding state south swept north elected president lincoln victory prompted seven southern slave state form confederate state america moved white house—no compromise reconciliation found regarding slavery secession subsequently april confederate attack fort sumter inspired north enthusiastically rally behind union leader moderate faction republican party lincoln confronted radical republican demanded harsher treatment south war democrat called compromise antiwar democrat called copperhead despised irreconcilable secessionist
